<ol><li>humanitarian

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гумно́</a> (24410)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gumьno</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гумно́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gumnó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гумна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гу́мна</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гу́мен</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гумён</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">agriculture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> threshing-floor, cleared plot of land in farms on which stacks of grain are piled, accompanied by threshing and processing of grain</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">agriculture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> barn, shed for compressed grain</li>
<li>a minced oath form of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">govnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гунн.html>гунн</a> (28514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Modern learned borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hunne</i>.
</p>

</p>

***гурьба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гурьба.html>гурьба́</a> (20905)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">hurma</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crowd</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гурьба.html>гурьба́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gurʹbá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гурьба.html>гурьбы́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crowd, throng</li></ol>

***гусеница.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гусеница.html>гу́сеница</a> (5591)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">юсеница</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jusenica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">гу́сениця</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">húsenycja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">гъсе́ница</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gǎsénica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">гу̏сеница</i>/<span class="Latn" lang="sh">gȕsenica</span>/<span class="Cyrl" lang="sh">гу̏сјеница</span>/<span class="Latn" lang="sh">gȕsjenica</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">gosẹ̑nica</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">housenka</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">husenica</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Polish language">Old Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-opl">wąsienica</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">gąsienica</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">husańca</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">guseńca</i>. Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ǫsěnica</i>. The initial <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>г</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">g</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>- is prothetic or by conflation with Common Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">гоущерица</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gušterica</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lizard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Russian <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ящерица.html>я́щерица</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jáščerica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), and is not related to Russian <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусь.html>гусь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gusʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусеница.html>гу́сеница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gúsenica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусеница.html>гу́сеницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусеница.html>гу́сеницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусеница.html>гу́сениц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>caterpillar</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mechanical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> caterpillar track</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">густꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gustyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gǫstъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***гусь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гусь.html>гусь</a> (4561)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gǫ̑sь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰh₂éns</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусь.html>гусь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gusʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусь.html>гу́ся</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусь.html>гу́си</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусь.html>гусе́й</a></b>)

<ol><li>goose

***гуща.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ща</a> (12887)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ща</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gušča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gǫšča</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gǫstъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ja</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ща</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gúšča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́щи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́щи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́щ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sediment, <i>(coffee)</i> grounds, <i>(beer)</i> lees, <i>soup</i> the body
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гадать.html>гада́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кофейный.html>кофе́йной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ще</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gadátʹ na koféjnoj gúšče</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to read the leaves, to make wild guesses (lit: tell fortunes by coffee grounds)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>thicket
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ще</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v gúšče lesá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">in the thick of the forest</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>thick, centre, middle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мую</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́щу</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:масса.html>ма́сс</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v sámuju <b>gúšču</b> mass</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">in the very midst of the masses</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ще</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:событие.html>собы́тий</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v samoj gúšče sobýtij</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">in the thick of things</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ща</a></b>

***да.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> (48)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*da</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">da</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>yes</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_5">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">da</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>and (сочинительный, <a href = vnd.unilang:соединительный.html>соедини́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:союз.html>сою́з</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:император.html>импера́тору</a> Карлу <a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>Вели́кому</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:недосуг.html>недосу́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писать</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On sam o sebé govoríl, što jemú, kak imperátoru Karlu Velikomu, nedosug učítʹsja čitátʹ <b>da</b> pisatʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He said of himself that he was like the Emperor Charlemagne, too busy to learn to read and write.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>but
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:граната.html>грана́ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́мы</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Da</b> granáty u nevó ne toj sistémy!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It's just - his grenades are the wrong caliber! (Quoted from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/White_Sun_of_the_Desert" class="extiw" title="w:White Sun of the Desert">White Sun of the Desert</a> after antagonist fails to obtain grenades.)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:расстаться.html>расста́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяц</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a>.<br />— <b><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— My s nej rasstálisʹ užé kak mésjac nazád.<br />— <b>Da</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">“We broke up like a month ago.”<br />“Really?”</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

***давать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> (162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dāvàti</i>. Composed as if from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">davátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give</li>
<li>to let, to allow</li>
<li>to hit, to strike, to clip</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put out, to consent to sex</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 13b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-да-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ва</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>дава́ться</a> (4619)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>дава́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">davátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:даться.html>да́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let oneself, to allow oneself (to be caught, to be cheated, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>дава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обида.html>оби́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>davátʹsja</b> v obídu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not to allow oneself to be pushed around/over</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come easily
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>дава́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:иностранный.html>иностра́нные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языки́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú ne <b>daválisʹ</b> inostránnyje jazykí.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Foreign languages didn't come easily to him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>.
